 Fadnavis has gone to the public through Jan Aashirwad Yatra

 ise pichley maheene tiz kiya gaya tha
 This feature aims to help 330 million active users read tweets according to their convenience
 yaad ke taur par bataa den twitor ne oktober main jaankaree di thi ki company ek bukmarking feechar develop kar rahaa he jisase twits ko seve kiya ja saktaa he
 According to IANS news, the company's product head Keith Coleman tweeted that the 'save for Letter' feature is doing great work
 company ke stoff product dijainer tina koyama ne guuruuvaar der raat ek twit main kaha, 'seve for letters' dal kii taraf se jari soochna! hamane apane feechar ko 'bukmarks' naam diya he, kyonki ye contate ko seve karne ke liye sabase prachlit turm he
 Also, it fits perfectly with the names of other navigation features

 After the election of 10 Rajya Sabha seats in Uttar Pradesh, now the Bari Legislative Council elections are held
 ek baar phir sattadhari bijepi or sapa-basapa gathbandhan sahit sara vipaksh aamane-saamne hoga
 Elections are to be held in 13 of the 38 legislative council seats to be elected by the state assembly members
 5 may ko inamen se 12 vidhaan parishad sadasyon kaa kaarykaal puraa ho rahe hai or ek seat pehle se rikt he
 The tenure of these members is coming to full term from the Legislative Council of Akhilesh Yadav, Rajendra Chaudhary, Naresh Uttam, Umar Ali Khan, Madhu Gupta, Ramsakal Gurjar and Vijay Yadav from Purnaspa
 bispi ke vijay pratap singh or sunil kumaar chittod, ralod ke choudhary mushtak, bijepi se mohsin raja or mahendra kumaar singh kaa bhi kaarykaal puraa ho rahaa he
 Apart from this, elections are to be held on the vacant seat of Ambika Chaudhary who went from SP to BSP
 is tarah se kul 13 vidhaan parishad siten khaali ho rahi hai
 The legislative council member has a total of 100 legislative council members in Mathematics
 inamen se vidhansabha sadasyon dwaara 38 vidhaan parishad sadasyon kaa chayan hota he
 There are 36 Legislative Council seats which are elected by the local body
 iske alaava 8 sadasyon kaa chunaav shikshakon dwaara or 8 sadsy snaatak sadasyon dwaara chune jate hai
 At the same time, 10 Legislative Council members are nominated
 in sabhi sadasyon kaa kaarykaal 6 saal ke liye hota he
 One-third of the members of the Legislative Council are elected every two years by legislators
 ek sadsy ke liye 31 vot kii jaruratvidhan parishad kii jin 13 siton kaa chunaav he, wo vidhayakon dwaara chune jane hai
 In this case, divide the total vacant seats by the total number of mlas, which will be achieved
 vahi sankhya ek vidhaan parishad sadsy ke liye chahie
 Uttar Pradesh has a total of 402 Legislative Assembly members and elections to 13 Legislative Council seats
 aise main 402 ko 13 se bhaag dete hai to kareeb 31 aata he
 Thus the votes of 31 mlas are required for one seat of the state
 bijepi ke 10, vipaksh do or 13veen seat ke liye ghamasanasoobe kii maujuuda vidhansabha main bijepi gathbandhan ke paas 324 vidhayak hai
 Apart from this, the figure of 331 comes from the combined rebel mlas of the SP-BSP and RLD along with the independent mlas
 aise main bijepi kii 10 seat par jeet tay he
 After this, 21 votes will be left extra
 aise main bijepi rajyasabha chunaav kii tarah 11waan ummidavaar maidan main utaar sakati he
 By joining the SP-BSP and Congress, the opposition can easily win two seats
 iske baad bhi uske 9 vot bachenge
 In such a situation, if the opposition field a third candidate, then the contest will be interesting like the Rajya Sabha elections
 vidhaan parishad or rajyasabha voting main antarasube kii 13 vidhaan parishad siton ke chunaav ke liye agle maheene april main adhisuchana jari ho sakati he
 Actually on May 5, the tenure of the members is being completed
 vidhaan parishad chunaav main vidhayak apana vot rajyasabha kii tarah poling agent ko dikhaane ke liye baadhya nahin hote hai
 In such a situation, cross voting is more likely
 aise main agar 13 seat par 14 ummidavaar maidan main aate hai to siyaasi ghamaasan dekhene ko phir milegaa

 Latitude is the name of the angular distance from the equator to the north or south pole of any place
 bumadhyarekha ko 0° kii akshansh rekha mana gaya he
 Important facts associated with latitude lines are as follows: (1) The imaginary lines drawn from west to east on the globe are called latitude lines
 inhen ansh main pradarshit kiya jaataa he
 (2) The number of latitude lines is 181
 (3)akshansh vah kone he, jo vishuvat rekha or kisi anya sthaan ke bich prithvi ke kendra par banati hai
 (4) The equator is considered to be in a zero degree position
 yahaan se uttar kii ore badhane vaali konik duuri ko uttari akshansh or dakshin kii duuri ko dakshini akshansh kehete hai
 (5) It has pole at its maximum limit, which is called 90 ° North latitude or Southern latitude
 (6)prithvi par kisi bhi desh yaa jagah kii sthiti kaa nirdhaaran us sthaan ke akshansh or deshaantar se hi hota he
 (7) All latitude lines are parallel
 (8)de akshanshen ke bich kii duuri jone ke naam se jaani jaati he
 (9) The distance between two latitudes is 111 km
 (10)bumadhya rekha ke uttar main 23 1° / 2 akshansh ko kark rekha mana gaya he, jabaki dakshin main 23 1° / 2 akshansh ko makar rekha mana gaya he

 iske saath hi saamaanya sardi, kaan main khont yaa phir kisi duusari vajah se jab kaan band ho jaataa haito dard hone lagata he

 agar kaan dard saamaanya str kaa he to aap in gharelu upayon se bhi use thik kar sakate hai

 Kartik month is considered to be a very holy month in Hinduism
 yah chaturmaas kaa antim maas he, isi maah se dev tatv majboot hota he
 In this month, experiments related to both money and religion are done
 isi maheene main tulsi kaa ropan or vivaah sarvottam hota he
 In this month, donating and donating lamps gives the auspicious results
 is burkarthikka maheenaa 25 oktober se 23 navambar tak rahegaa
 In the month of Kartik, there is food and livelihood? - From this month it is advisable to eat balsamic things, and dry fruits - things that are hot in nature and keep energy for a long time, such things should be eaten- In this month, pulse ( Pulses) Eating is forbidden - Bathing of sun rays is also considered better than this month- Sleeping in afternoon is also forbidden in this month
 What is the relation of wealth of Kartik month? This month is very dear to Shri Hari, so Mother Lakshmi is also very dear - this month Lord Vishnu wakes up from yoga sleep and there is a rain of joy and grace in the creation - In this month Mother Lakshmi travels on earth, and It gives immense wealth to the devotees - this month only to get the blessings of Maa Lakshmi
 Deepawali and Gopashtami are celebrated - by using special worship and use this month, you can get immense wealth for the time to come and be free from debt and losses
 a big festival like Diwali is celebrated for the blessings of Lakshmi - yet every day in Kartik month, measures should be taken to get the blessings of Mother Lakshmi - In Kartik month Worship Lord Vishnu and Lakshmi ji daily at night - worship in pink or shiny cloth - if you want money, then with a garland of lotus leaves, if you want to pay off debt, then if you want to earn money in business, then garland of conch Chant at least 3 beads of the mantra - the mantra is "om Shree Lakshmi Vasudevaya Namah" After the end of Kartik month, keep this garland in place of your wealth
